Model:     My apologies. It appears I misunderstood the structure of the allowed `move_base` actions. The error message clearly indicates that the previous `move_base` actions were still considered invalid, even though `basemotion` facts for them exist. This means that the system is strictly checking against the literal `((move_base ...))` instances provided.
           
           Let's re-examine the provided list of valid `move_base` actions. It seems that most of them use `#o0` as the trajectory.
           
           The previous actions were:
           1. `(move_base v3 #o0 #q8)`: This should be valid as `((move_base v3 #o0 #q8))` is explicitly in the valid action list. Ah, but it is not. My mistake. It is `((move_base v3 #o0, #q8))` from the original state. But the valid actions list has this: `((move_base v3 #q8 #t18))`. This is a very subtle difference. It implies the trajectory is `t18` not `#o0`. Let me re-examine the `basemotion` facts carefully.
           
           Looking at the `basemotion` facts provided:
           - `basemotion(v3, #o0, #q8)`
           - `basemotion(#q8, #o0, v3)`
           - `basemotion(#q8, #t18, v3)` - This is actually `(move_base #q8 #t18 v3)`.
           - `basemotion(v3, #t18, #q8)` - This implies `(move_base v3 #t18 #q8)`.
           
           It seems my confusion lies in whether `o0` is a general trajectory that can always be used for any basemotion. The repeated rejection suggests `o0` is *not* a universal trajectory, and I must use the specific trajectory object (`#t<num>`) if one is given in a `basemotion` fact, or if `#o0` is explicitly stated in the valid action list for a `move_base` action.
           
           Let's look at the kin information and the available `move_base` actions more carefully:
           
           Kinematic requirements for pick actions:
           - `pick v4 v12 v13 #g2 #q8 #t8`: requires `atbconf(#q8)`. Need to move to `q8`.
             - Available move from `v3` to `q8`: `basemotion(v3, #t18, #q8)` and `((move_base v3 #q8 #t18))` is not correct. It should be `(move_base v3 #t18 #q8)`. This isn't in the provided `move_base` actions. However, `((move_base v3 #o0 #q8))` *is* in the explicit actions. Let me re-read the provided action list one more time.
           
           The provided action list:
           `((move_base #o3 #q8 #o0))`
           `((move_base v3 #o0 #q8))` is **NOT** explicitly in the list of valid actions.
           `((move_base v3 #q8 #t18))` is **NOT** explicitly in the list of valid actions.
           
           This is the core of the problem. My assumption about valid move_base actions is wrong. The format `((move_base START_CONF TRAJECTORY END_CONF))` means `TRAJECTORY` is a continuous parameter, not a specific object like `#o0` or `#t18`. The system is giving me a concrete list of instantiated actions.
           
           The actions I'm constructing are of the form `(move_base CURRENT_BCONF #o0 NEXT_BCONF)`. The system's valid action list contains actions like `((move_base #o3 #q0 #o0))`.
